## 1. Design Philosophy

### 1.1 Core Principles

| Principle | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| **Focus First** | Reduce noise, surface what matters. Smart categorization over manual sorting. |
| **Fluid Interactions** | Glass morphism with liquid animations. Every action feels natural and responsive. |
| **Contextual Intelligence** | AI assistance appears when helpful, never intrusive. Learn from behavior. |
| **Unified Experience** | Email and calendar are deeply integrated, not separate apps. |
| **Zero Friction** | Common actions require minimal clicks. Keyboard-first for power users. |

### 1.3 Color System

| Element | Light Mode | Dark Mode | Purpose |
|---------|------------|-----------|---------|
| Primary Accent | `#0A84FF` | `#0A84FF` | Actions, links, selection |
| Priority | `#FFD60A` | `#FFD60A` | Priority senders, stars |
| Success | `#30D158` | `#30D158` | Sent, accepted |
| Warning | `#FF9F0A` | `#FF9F0A` | Gatekeeper, pending |
| Destructive | `#FF453A` | `#FF453A` | Delete, decline |
| Unread | `#007AFF` | `#64D2FF` | Unread indicator |
| Muted | `#8E8E93` | `#636366` | Secondary text, timestamps |

### 1.4 Account Color Coding

Each connected account gets a unique accent color for visual distinction:

```
Account 1 (mario@gmail.com):     â— Blue    #0A84FF
Account 2 (mario@work.com):      â— Purple  #BF5AF2
```

### 2.2 View Modes

| Mode | Description | Use Case |
|------|-------------|----------|
| **Smart Inbox** | AI-categorized sections | Daily email triage |
| **Traditional** | Single chronological list | Users who prefer classic view |
| **Focused** | Priority only, everything else hidden | Deep work sessions |
| **Search Results** | Filtered view from search | Finding specific emails |
| **Label View** | Emails with specific label | Project-based organization |

## 3. Core Email Workflows

### 3.1 Inbox Zero Flow

**Goal**: Help users achieve inbox zero through systematic triage.


**Quick Actions (Swipe/Keyboard)**:
| Action | Swipe Left | Swipe Right | Keyboard |
|--------|------------|-------------|----------|
| Archive | Short swipe | - | `e` |
| Delete | Long swipe | - | `#` |
| Snooze | - | Short swipe | `b` |
| Star | - | Long swipe | `s` |

### 3.3 Compose Email

**Trigger Points**:
- Floating Action Button (mobile)
- Keyboard shortcut `c`
- "Compose" button in sidebar
- Reply/Forward from thread

### 5.3 Smart Categorization

**How it works**:

| Category | Detection Signals |
|----------|-------------------|
| **Primary** | From contacts, direct replies, person-to-person |
| **Newsletters** | `List-Unsubscribe` header, bulk sender patterns, "unsubscribe" in footer |
| **Notifications** | `noreply@`, transactional patterns, app notifications |

**User Override**:
```

Visual States:
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
â€¢ Unread: Bold sender/subject, blue left border (4px)
â€¢ Priority: Yellow star, subtle yellow background tint
â€¢ Snoozed: Clock icon, muted text, "Snoozed until..." subtitle
â€¢ Selected: Primary accent background
â€¢ Hover: Reveal quick actions, subtle elevation
â€¢ Has attachment: Paperclip icon with count
â€¢ Newsletter: Newspaper icon
â€¢ Notification: Bell icon
```

## 7. Interaction Patterns

### 7.1 Keyboard Shortcuts

| Category | Shortcut | Action |
|----------|----------|--------|
| **Navigation** | `j` / `â†“` | Next thread |
| | `k` / `â†‘` | Previous thread |
| | `o` / `Enter` | Open thread |
| | `u` | Back to list |
| | `g` then `i` | Go to Inbox |
| | `g` then `s` | Go to Starred |
| | `g` then `d` | Go to Drafts |
| | `g` then `t` | Go to Sent |
| **Actions** | `c` | Compose new |
| | `r` | Reply |
| | `a` | Reply all |
| | `f` | Forward |
| | `e` | Archive |
| | `#` | Delete |
| | `s` | Star/Unstar |
| | `b` | Snooze |
| | `l` | Label |
| | `v` | Move to folder |
| **Selection** | `x` | Select thread |
| | `* a` | Select all |
| | `* n` | Deselect all |
| | `* r` | Select read |
| | `* u` | Select unread |
| **Search** | `/` | Focus search |
| | `Esc` | Clear/close |
| **Other** | `?` | Show shortcuts |
| | `Cmd/Ctrl + Enter` | Send email |

### 7.3 Drag & Drop

| Source | Target | Action |
|--------|--------|--------|
| Email thread | Label in sidebar | Apply label |
| Email thread | Folder in sidebar | Move to folder |
| Email thread | Trash | Delete |
| File from desktop | Compose window | Attach file |
| Calendar event | Different time slot | Reschedule |

## 8. Responsive Behavior

### 8.1 Breakpoints

| Breakpoint | Width | Layout |
|------------|-------|--------|
| Mobile | < 640px | Single column, bottom nav |
| Tablet | 640px - 1024px | Two columns (sidebar + list OR list + detail) |
| Desktop | > 1024px | Three columns |
| Large Desktop | > 1440px | Three columns with wider reading pane |

---

## 9. Accessibility

### 9.1 Screen Reader Support

| Element | ARIA Role | Announcement |
|---------|-----------|--------------|
| Thread list | `listbox` | "Email list, 25 conversations" |
| Thread item | `option` | "From John Smith, Subject: Project Proposal, unread, has 2 attachments" |
| Message | `article` | "Message from John Smith, sent January 21 at 10:30 AM" |
| Compose | `dialog` | "New message dialog" |
| Search | `searchbox` | "Search emails" |

### 9.2 Focus Management

```
Tab Order:
1. Search bar
2. Compose button
3. Navigation folders
4. Thread list
5. Thread actions
6. Message content
7. Reply box

Focus Indicators:
- 2px solid primary accent
- High contrast in both light/dark modes
- Never removed, only styled
```

### 9.3 Color Contrast

| Element | Light Mode | Dark Mode | Ratio |
|---------|------------|-----------|-------|
| Primary text | #1C1C1E | #FFFFFF | 15.8:1 |
| Secondary text | #636366 | #EBEBF5 | 7.2:1 |
| Links/Actions | #007AFF | #0A84FF | 4.5:1+ |
| Error text | #FF3B30 | #FF453A | 4.5:1+ |

### 9.4 Reduced Motion

```css
@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
  * {
    animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
    transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
  }
}
```

When reduced motion is enabled:
- Instant state changes instead of animations
- No parallax or scroll effects
- Static loading indicators instead of spinners

---


## Animation Tokens Reference

```typescript
// src/styles/sparkles-animations.ts

export const sparklesAnimations = {
  // Durations
  instant: '0ms',
  fast: '150ms',
  normal: '250ms',
  slow: '400ms',

  // Easings
  easeOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.0, 0.0, 0.2, 1)',
  easeIn: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0.0, 1, 1)',
  easeInOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0.0, 0.2, 1)',
  spring: 'cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.275)',
  bounce: 'cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)',

  // Framer Motion Presets
  threadSlide: {
    initial: { opacity: 0, x: -20 },
    animate: { opacity: 1, x: 0 },
    exit: { opacity: 0, x: 20 },
    transition: { duration: 0.25, ease: [0.0, 0.0, 0.2, 1] }
  },

  modalScale: {
    initial: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 },
    animate: { opacity: 1, scale: 1 },
    exit: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 },
    transition: { type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }
  },

  listStagger: {
    animate: { transition: { staggerChildren: 0.05 } }
  },

  toast: {
    initial: { opacity: 0, y: 50 },
    animate: { opacity: 1, y: 0 },
    exit: { opacity: 0, y: 20 },
    transition: { type: 'spring', damping: 20, stiffness: 300 }
  }
};
```

---

---

## 11. LiquidMenu Bar Integration

Sparkles integrates deeply with the LiquidMenuBar, providing context-aware menus, status indicators, and quick actions that mirror the native macOS Spark Mail experience.

### 11.1 Menu Bar Registration

When Sparkles is active, it registers its identity and custom menus via `useAppMenuBar`:

```typescript
// src/components/features/sparkles/hooks/useSparklesMenuBar.ts

import { useAppMenuBar } from '@/components/menu-bar';
import { Mail, Inbox, Send, Archive, Trash2, Clock, Star, Search, Tag, Calendar } from 'lucide-react';

export function useSparklesMenuBar() {
  useAppMenuBar({
    appName: 'Sparkles',
    appIcon: Mail,
    menus: [
      sparklesMailboxMenu,
      sparklesMessageMenu,
      sparklesFormatMenu,
    ],
    statusIcons: [
      syncStatusIcon,
      unreadCountIcon,
      gatekeeperIcon,
    ],
    privacyIndicators: {
      // No special privacy indicators for email
    }
  });
}
```

### 11.2 Menu Structure

#### Menu Bar Layout

When Sparkles is active, the menu bar shows:

**Settings Sections:**

| Section | Contents |
|---------|----------|
| **General** | Default account, reading pane, preview lines, behavior |
| **Accounts** | Manage connected accounts, sync settings, signatures |
| **Notifications** | Push notifications, sounds, badge settings |
| **Signatures** | Per-account email signatures |
| **Smart Inbox** | Category preferences, priority sender management |
| **Gatekeeper** | Screening mode, blocked senders list, whitelist |
| **Templates** | Saved email templates for quick compose |
| **Rules** | Auto-filing rules, filters |
| **Shortcuts** | Keyboard shortcut customization |
| **Privacy** | Remote image loading, tracking protection |
| **Advanced** | Sync frequency, cache, debug options |

#### Accounts Management Panel

When "Add Account..." or "Accounts > Account Settings..." is selected:


### 11.5 Right Zone Status Icons

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ âœ¦ Sparkles â”‚ Mailbox â”‚ Message â”‚...â”‚     [ğŸ”„] [ğŸ›¡ï¸5] [ğŸ“¬12] â”‚ ğŸ”” â”‚ â˜€ï¸ â”‚ âš™ï¸ â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
                                              â”‚     â”‚      â”‚
                                              â”‚     â”‚      â””â”€â”€ Unread count badge
                                              â”‚     â””â”€â”€ Gatekeeper pending (orange)
                                              â””â”€â”€ Sync status (spinning when syncing)
```

**Status Icons Specification:**

| Icon | ID | Purpose | States | Click Action |
|------|-----|---------|--------|--------------|
| ğŸ”„ | `sparkles-sync` | Sync indicator | Idle (gray), Syncing (spinning blue), Error (red) | Force sync |
| ğŸ›¡ï¸ | `sparkles-gatekeeper` | Gatekeeper pending | Hidden (0), Orange badge (>0) | Open Gatekeeper panel |
| ğŸ“¬ | `sparkles-unread` | Unread count | Hidden (0), Blue badge (>0) | Go to Inbox |

```typescript
// Status icon definitions
const statusIcons: StatusIconDef[] = [
  {
    id: 'sparkles-sync',
    icon: RefreshCw,
    color: syncStatus === 'syncing' ? 'var(--system-blue)' :
           syncStatus === 'error' ? 'var(--system-red)' :
           'var(--glass-text-tertiary)',
    tooltip: syncStatus === 'syncing' ? 'Syncing mail...' :
             syncStatus === 'error' ? 'Sync failed - click to retry' :
             'All mail synced',
    onClick: () => syncAllMail(),
    priority: 10,
  },
  {
    id: 'sparkles-gatekeeper',
    icon: Shield,
    color: pendingCount > 0 ? 'var(--system-orange)' : 'var(--glass-text-tertiary)',
    tooltip: pendingCount > 0 ? `${pendingCount} senders awaiting review` : 'Gatekeeper: No pending senders',
    onClick: () => openGatekeeper(),
    priority: 20,
    // Badge rendered via custom component
  },
  {
    id: 'sparkles-unread',
    icon: Mail,
    color: unreadCount > 0 ? 'var(--system-blue)' : 'var(--glass-text-tertiary)',
    tooltip: unreadCount > 0 ? `${unreadCount} unread emails` : 'No unread emails',
    onClick: () => goToInbox(),
    priority: 30,
  },
];
```

### 11.6 Keyboard Shortcuts Reference

The menu bar displays keyboard shortcuts for all actions. Here's the complete map:

| Category | Action | Shortcut | Menu Location |
|----------|--------|----------|---------------|
| **App** | Settings | `âŒ˜,` | Sparkles |
| | Command Center | `âŒ˜K` | Sparkles |
| | Hide Sparkles | `âŒ˜H` | Sparkles |
| | Hide Others | `âŒ¥âŒ˜H` | Sparkles |
| | Quit | `âŒ˜Q` | Sparkles |
| **Navigation** | Smart Inbox | `âŒ˜1` | Go |
| | Gatekeeper | `âŒ˜2` | Go |
| | Inbox | `âŒ˜3` | Go |
| | Sent | `âŒ˜4` | Go |
| | Drafts | `âŒ˜5` | Go |
| | Snoozed | `âŒ˜6` | Go |
| | Scheduled | `âŒ˜7` | Go |
| | Starred | `âŒ˜8` | Go |
| | Trash | `âŒ˜9` | Go |
| | Previous Message | `âŒ˜[` | Go |
| | Next Message | `âŒ˜]` | Go |
| | Calendar | `âŒ˜â‡§C` | Go |
| **Compose** | New Message | `âŒ˜N` | Message |
| | Reply | `âŒ˜R` | Message |
| | Reply All | `â‡§âŒ˜R` | Message |
| | Forward | `âŒ˜J` | Message |
| **Actions** | Archive | `âŒ˜E` | Message |
| | Delete | `âŒ«` | Message |
| | Toggle Star | `âŒ˜S` | Message |
| | Mark Unread | `â‡§âŒ˜U` | Message |
| | Mark Read | `âŒ˜U` | Message |
| | Snooze | `âŒ˜B` | Message |
| | Mute Thread | `âŒ˜M` | Message |
| **View** | Toggle Sidebar | `âŒ˜\` | View |
| | Toggle Reading Pane | `â‡§âŒ˜R` | View |
| | Refresh | `âŒ˜R` | View |
| **Search** | Focus Search | `âŒ˜F` or `/` | â€” |
| **Mailbox** | Get All New Mail | `â‡§âŒ˜N` | Mailbox |

### 11.7 Implementation Hook

```typescript
// src/components/features/sparkles/hooks/useSparklesMenuBar.ts

import { useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
import { useAppMenuBar } from '@/components/menu-bar';
import { useSparklesStore } from '@/stores/sparklesStore';
import {
  Mail, Inbox, Send, Archive, Trash2, Clock, Star, Search,
  Tag, Calendar, Shield, RefreshCw, Reply, Forward, Mute,
  Bold, Italic, Underline, Link, Image, Sparkles as SparklesIcon,
  Settings, Users, UserPlus, Eye, EyeOff, Command, LogOut, Power,
  Info, Share2
} from 'lucide-react';
import type { MenuDef, MenuItemDef, StatusIconDef } from '@/components/menu-bar';

export function useSparklesMenuBar() {
  const {
    accounts,
    activeAccountId,
    syncStatus,
    unreadCount,
    pendingSenderCount,
    activeFolder,
    gatekeeperMode,
    viewMode,
    readingPanePosition,
    selectedThread,
  } = useSparklesStore();

  // Actions
  const openSettings = useCallback(() => {/* Open settings modal */}, []);
  const openTeams = useCallback(() => {/* Open teams management */}, []);
  const openAccounts = useCallback(() => {/* Open accounts panel */}, []);
  const addAccount = useCallback(() => {/* Start OAuth flow */}, []);
  const addSharedAccount = useCallback(() => {/* Add delegated mailbox */}, []);
  const openCommandCenter = useCallback(() => {/* Open command palette */}, []);
  const logOut = useCallback(() => {/* Sign out all accounts */}, []);
  const quitSparkles = useCallback(() => {/* Close panel */}, []);
  const syncAllMail = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const openGatekeeper = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const goToInbox = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const compose = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const reply = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const replyAll = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const forward = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const archive = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const deleteThread = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const toggleStar = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const snooze = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);
  const muteThread = useCallback(() => {/* ... */}, []);

  // Sparkles App Menu (extends/overrides the âœ¦ Liquid Menu)
  const sparklesAppMenu: MenuDef = useMemo(() => ({
    id: 'sparkles-app',
    label: 'Sparkles',
    items: [
      {
        id: 'about',
        label: 'About Sparkles',
        icon: Info,
        action: () => openAboutDialog(),
      },
      { id: 'div-about', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'settings',
        label: 'Settings...',
        icon: Settings,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜,',
        action: openSettings,
      },
      { id: 'div-settings', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'teams',
        label: 'Teams...',
        icon: Users,
        action: openTeams,
      },
      { id: 'div-teams', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'accounts',
        label: 'Accounts',
        icon: Mail,
        submenu: [
          // Dynamic account list
          ...accounts.map((account, index) => ({
            id: `account-${account.id}`,
            label: account.email,
            checked: account.id === activeAccountId,
            action: () => setActiveAccount(account.id),
            submenu: [
              {
                id: `account-${account.id}-all`,
                label: 'All Folders',
                checked: account.syncMode === 'all',
                action: () => setAccountSyncMode(account.id, 'all'),
              },
              {
                id: `account-${account.id}-inbox`,
                label: 'Inbox Only',
                checked: account.syncMode === 'inbox',
                action: () => setAccountSyncMode(account.id, 'inbox'),
              },
              {
                id: `account-${account.id}-disable`,
                label: 'Disable Account',
                checked: !account.isEnabled,
                action: () => toggleAccountEnabled(account.id),
              },
            ],
          })),
          { id: 'div-accounts', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
          {
            id: 'account-settings',
            label: 'Account Settings...',
            icon: Settings,
            action: openAccounts,
          },
        ],
      },
      { id: 'div-accounts-main', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'add-account',
        label: 'Add Account...',
        icon: UserPlus,
        action: addAccount,
      },
      {
        id: 'add-shared-account',
        label: 'Add Shared Account...',
        icon: Share2,
        action: addSharedAccount,
      },
      { id: 'div-add', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'services',
        label: 'Services',
        submenu: [], // Populated by system
      },
      { id: 'div-services', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'hide',
        label: 'Hide Sparkles',
        icon: EyeOff,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜H',
        action: () => hideWindow(),
      },
      {
        id: 'hide-others',
        label: 'Hide Others',
        shortcut: 'âŒ¥âŒ˜H',
        action: () => hideOthers(),
      },
      {
        id: 'show-all',
        label: 'Show All',
        icon: Eye,
        action: () => showAll(),
        disabled: true, // Enabled when windows are hidden
      },
      { id: 'div-hide', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'command-center',
        label: 'Command Center',
        icon: Command,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜K',
        action: openCommandCenter,
      },
      { id: 'div-command', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'logout',
        label: 'Log Out',
        icon: LogOut,
        action: logOut,
      },
      { id: 'div-logout', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'quit',
        label: 'Quit Sparkles',
        icon: Power,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜Q',
        action: quitSparkles,
        danger: true,
      },
    ],
  }), [accounts, activeAccountId, openSettings, openTeams, openAccounts, addAccount, addSharedAccount, openCommandCenter, logOut, quitSparkles]);

  // Mailbox Menu
  const mailboxMenu: MenuDef = useMemo(() => ({
    id: 'sparkles-mailbox',
    label: 'Mailbox',
    items: [
      {
        id: 'get-mail',
        label: 'Get All New Mail',
        icon: RefreshCw,
        shortcut: 'â‡§âŒ˜N',
        action: syncAllMail,
      },
      { id: 'div-1', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'gatekeeper',
        label: 'Gatekeeper',
        icon: Shield,
        submenu: [
          {
            id: 'review-pending',
            label: `Review Pending (${pendingSenderCount})`,
            icon: Shield,
            action: openGatekeeper,
            disabled: pendingSenderCount === 0,
          },
          { id: 'div-gk', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
          {
            id: 'gk-before',
            label: 'Screen Before Inbox',
            checked: gatekeeperMode === 'before_inbox',
            action: () => setGatekeeperMode('before_inbox'),
          },
          {
            id: 'gk-inside',
            label: 'Screen Inside Inbox',
            checked: gatekeeperMode === 'inside_inbox',
            action: () => setGatekeeperMode('inside_inbox'),
          },
          {
            id: 'gk-disabled',
            label: 'Accept All Senders',
            checked: gatekeeperMode === 'disabled',
            action: () => setGatekeeperMode('disabled'),
          },
        ],
      },
      { id: 'div-2', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'sync-all',
        label: 'Synchronize All',
        icon: RefreshCw,
        action: syncAllMail,
      },
    ],
  }), [pendingSenderCount, gatekeeperMode, syncAllMail, openGatekeeper]);

  // Message Menu
  const messageMenu: MenuDef = useMemo(() => ({
    id: 'sparkles-message',
    label: 'Message',
    items: [
      {
        id: 'new-message',
        label: 'New Message',
        icon: Mail,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜N',
        action: compose,
      },
      { id: 'div-1', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'reply',
        label: 'Reply',
        icon: Reply,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜R',
        action: reply,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
      },
      {
        id: 'reply-all',
        label: 'Reply All',
        shortcut: 'â‡§âŒ˜R',
        action: replyAll,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
      },
      {
        id: 'forward',
        label: 'Forward',
        icon: Forward,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜J',
        action: forward,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
      },
      { id: 'div-2', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'archive',
        label: 'Archive',
        icon: Archive,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜E',
        action: archive,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
      },
      {
        id: 'delete',
        label: 'Delete',
        icon: Trash2,
        shortcut: 'âŒ«',
        action: deleteThread,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
        danger: true,
      },
      { id: 'div-3', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'toggle-star',
        label: 'Toggle Star',
        icon: Star,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜S',
        action: toggleStar,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
      },
      { id: 'div-4', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'snooze',
        label: 'Snooze...',
        icon: Clock,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜B',
        action: snooze,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
        submenu: [
          { id: 'snooze-later', label: 'Later Today (3:00 PM)', action: () => snoozeUntil('later') },
          { id: 'snooze-tonight', label: 'Tonight (8:00 PM)', action: () => snoozeUntil('tonight') },
          { id: 'snooze-tomorrow', label: 'Tomorrow (8:00 AM)', action: () => snoozeUntil('tomorrow') },
          { id: 'snooze-weekend', label: 'This Weekend', action: () => snoozeUntil('weekend') },
          { id: 'snooze-nextweek', label: 'Next Week', action: () => snoozeUntil('nextweek') },
          { id: 'div-snooze', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
          { id: 'snooze-custom', label: 'Pick Date & Time...', action: () => openSnoozePicker() },
        ],
      },
      {
        id: 'mute',
        label: 'Mute Thread',
        icon: Mute,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜M',
        action: muteThread,
        disabled: !selectedThread,
      },
    ],
  }), [selectedThread, compose, reply, replyAll, forward, archive, deleteThread, toggleStar, snooze, muteThread]);

  // Format Menu (only shown when composing)
  const formatMenu: MenuDef = useMemo(() => ({
    id: 'sparkles-format',
    label: 'Format',
    items: [
      {
        id: 'style',
        label: 'Style',
        submenu: [
          { id: 'bold', label: 'Bold', icon: Bold, shortcut: 'âŒ˜B', action: () => formatText('bold') },
          { id: 'italic', label: 'Italic', icon: Italic, shortcut: 'âŒ˜I', action: () => formatText('italic') },
          { id: 'underline', label: 'Underline', icon: Underline, shortcut: 'âŒ˜U', action: () => formatText('underline') },
        ],
      },
      { id: 'div-1', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'add-link',
        label: 'Add Link...',
        icon: Link,
        shortcut: 'âŒ˜K',
        action: () => insertLink(),
      },
      {
        id: 'insert-image',
        label: 'Insert Image...',
        icon: Image,
        action: () => insertImage(),
      },
      { id: 'div-2', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
      {
        id: 'ai-improve',
        label: 'AI Improve Writing',
        icon: SparklesIcon,
        submenu: [
          { id: 'ai-professional', label: 'Make Professional', action: () => aiImprove('professional') },
          { id: 'ai-casual', label: 'Make Casual', action: () => aiImprove('casual') },
          { id: 'ai-shorter', label: 'Make Shorter', action: () => aiImprove('shorter') },
          { id: 'ai-longer', label: 'Make Longer', action: () => aiImprove('longer') },
          { id: 'ai-grammar', label: 'Fix Grammar', action: () => aiImprove('grammar') },
          { id: 'div-ai', label: '', dividerAfter: true },
          { id: 'ai-custom', label: 'Custom Prompt...', action: () => openAIPrompt() },
        ],
      },
    ],
  }), []);

  // Status Icons
  const statusIcons: StatusIconDef[] = useMemo(() => [
    {
      id: 'sparkles-sync',
      icon: RefreshCw,
      color: syncStatus === 'syncing' ? 'var(--system-blue)' :
             syncStatus === 'error' ? 'var(--system-red)' :
             'var(--glass-text-tertiary)',
      tooltip: syncStatus === 'syncing' ? 'Syncing mail...' :
               syncStatus === 'error' ? 'Sync failed - click to retry' :
               'All mail synced',
      onClick: syncAllMail,
      priority: 10,
    },
    {
      id: 'sparkles-gatekeeper',
      icon: Shield,
      color: pendingSenderCount > 0 ? 'var(--system-orange)' : 'var(--glass-text-tertiary)',
      tooltip: pendingSenderCount > 0
        ? `${pendingSenderCount} senders awaiting review`
        : 'Gatekeeper: No pending senders',
      onClick: openGatekeeper,
      priority: 20,
    },
    {
      id: 'sparkles-unread',
      icon: Mail,
      color: unreadCount > 0 ? 'var(--system-blue)' : 'var(--glass-text-tertiary)',
      tooltip: unreadCount > 0 ? `${unreadCount} unread emails` : 'No unread emails',
      onClick: goToInbox,
      priority: 30,
    },
  ], [syncStatus, pendingSenderCount, unreadCount, syncAllMail, openGatekeeper, goToInbox]);

  // Register with menu bar
  useAppMenuBar({
    appName: 'Sparkles',
    appIcon: Mail,
    menus: [sparklesAppMenu, mailboxMenu, messageMenu, formatMenu],
    statusIcons,
  });
}
```

### 11.9 Context-Aware Menu States

The menu items dynamically enable/disable based on context:

| Context | Affected Items | State |
|---------|---------------|-------|
| No thread selected | Reply, Forward, Archive, Delete, Star, Snooze, Mute | Disabled |
| Thread selected | Reply, Forward, Archive, Delete, Star, Snooze, Mute | Enabled |
| Composing email | Format menu items | Enabled |
| Not composing | Format menu items | Hidden or Disabled |
| Gatekeeper has pending | Review Pending | Shows count, Enabled |
| Gatekeeper empty | Review Pending (0) | Disabled |
| Syncing | Sync icon | Blue, Spinning |
| Sync error | Sync icon | Red, Static |
| Has unread | Unread icon | Blue with badge |
| No unread | Unread icon | Gray, no badge |

### 11.10 Animation & Feedback

**Menu Dropdowns:**
- Use `MenuDropdown` primitive with Framer Motion
- 150ms ease-out entrance
- Backdrop blur matches glass hierarchy

**Status Icon Interactions:**
- Hover: Subtle scale (1.05) + tooltip
- Active/Syncing: CSS animation for rotation
- Badge: Pulse animation on count change

```typescript
// Badge pulse animation
const badgePulse = {
  initial: { scale: 1 },
  animate: {
    scale: [1, 1.2, 1],
    transition: { duration: 0.3 }
  }
};
```
